=== SQL #7 ===

Overall Stats
=============
        Buffer       Execution                     Total         Elapsed         SQL        Plan
          Gets           Count     Gets/Exec     Gets(%)         Time(s)  Hash Value  Hash Value  Module
--------------  --------------  ------------  ----------  --------------  ----------  ----------  --------------------
 5,766,455,073      12,911,525        446.61       46.56      133,118.31  1109436699   260787314  JDBC Thin Client@jsintws01p
 
SQL Text
========
SELECT CASE WHEN T_ALL  = T_CNT1 THEN '01'  -- 전부   승인이면   승인
                WHEN T_ALL  = T_CNT2 THEN '02'  -- 전부 불승인이면 불승인
                WHEN T_CNT3 > 0      THEN '03'  -- 보류 1개이상시 보류
                WHEN T_CNT4 > 0      THEN '90'  -- 반려 1개이상시 반려
                WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003'
                 AND T_CNT5 > 0      THEN '02'  -- 공동주택아니고 30임미만 1개이상시 불승인
                WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003'
                 AND T_CNT6 > 0      THEN '02'  -- 공동주택아니고 최저임금 1개이상시 불승인
                WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD <> '6003'
                 AND T_CNT1 > 0
                 AND T_CNT5 = 0
                 AND T_CNT6 = 0      THEN '01'  -- 공동주택아니고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이고 최저임금, 30민미만이 없으면 승인(일부승인)
                WHEN MINWON_DOC_CD  = '6003'
                 AND T_CNT1 > 0      THEN '01'  -- 공동주택이고 지원원별 승인 1개이상이면 승인(일부승인)
                ELSE '00'                       -- 해당하는 조건 없음
           END    AS RESULT
      
      FROM (SELECT COUNT(C.JEOPSU_NO) AS T_ALL                                                            -- 전체
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('01','04') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT1  -- 승인
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT2  -- 불승인
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD IN ('03','06') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT3  -- 보류
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_SIMSA_RESULT_CD  = '90'        THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT4  -- 반려
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.MN30_MIMAN_FG             IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT5  -- 30인미만임금 불승인건
                 , SUM(CASE WHEN A.CHOEJEO_IMGEUM_FG         IN ('02','05') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS T_CNT6  -- 최저임금     불승인건
                 , MAX(B.MINWON_DOC_CD) AS MINWON_DOC_CD                                                  -- 민원서식
                 , MIN(A.SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD) AS SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD                            -- 심사진행상태
              FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT A
              JOIN US_IOWN.IAA100MT C
                ON C.ILJARI_NO = A.ILJARI_NO
              LEFT OUTER
              JOIN US_IOWN.IQA500MT B
                ON B.JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO
             WHERE A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = :B1          -- 대표일자리번호
               AND A.JIWON_YEAR       = :B2
               AND A.JEONGGI_CNT      = :B3
               AND A.SIMSA_CNT        = (SELECT MAX(Z.SIMSA_CNT)
                                           FROM US_IOWN.IJB050MT Z
                                          WHERE Z.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                                            AND Z.JIWON_YEAR       = A.JIWON_YEAR
                                            AND Z.JEONGGI_CNT      = A.JEONGGI_CNT
                                      )
           )

INSERT INTO IKA050MT_IFS (
               EAI_JEONSONG_SER
             , DAESANG_DATE
             , TOTAL_COUNT
             , DAY_COUNT
             , COUNT_RATE
             , INSERT_DATE
             , EAI_DML_YUHYEONG
             , EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI
             , EAI_JEONSONG_YN 
             )
            SELECT SQ_EIS_DAILY_JOB_SER.NEXTVAL                             AS EAI_JEONSONG_SER
                 , TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD')        AS DAESANG_DATE
                 , Y.NJ_CNT                                                 AS TOTAL_COUNT
                 , Y.DI_CNT                                                 AS DAY_COUNT
                 , DECODE(Y.BEF_CNT, 0, 0, NVL(ROUND(((Y.DI_CNT - Y.BEF_CNT)/Y.BEF_CNT)*100, 2), 0)) AS JG_CNT_PCT
                 , SYSDATE                                                  AS INSERT_DATE
                 , DECODE(NVL(Y.TODAY_YN, 'I'), 'Y', 'U', 'I')              AS EAI_DML_YUHYEONG
                 , SYSDATE                                                  AS EAI_SAENGSEONG_ILSI
                 , 'N'                                                      AS EAI_JEONSONG_YN
              FROM (SELECT ZZ.DT
                         , NVL(MAX(NJ_CNT),0) NJ_CNT
                         , NVL(MAX(DI_CNT),0) DI_CNT
                         , NVL(MAX(BEF_CNT),0) BEF_CNT
                         , (SELECT 'Y' FROM IKA050MT_IFS C WHERE C.DAESANG_DATE = TO_DATE(TO_CHAR(SYSDATE, 'YYYYMMDD'), 'YYYYMMDD') AND ROWNUM = 1) AS TODAY_YN
                      FROM (
                            SELECT '1'
                                 , TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') AS DT
                                 , COUNT(DISTINCT AA.ILJARI_NO ||AA.GEUNROJA_NO) AS NJ_CNT
                                 , 0 AS DI_CNT
                                 , 0 AS BEF_CNT
                              FROM (SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO 
                                      FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM IBC250MT
                                             WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                             GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                           ) C
                                         , IBB010MT D
                                         , IBB020MT E
                                     WHERE D.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND E.JEOPSU_NO = D.JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND E.ILJARI_NO = D.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND E.JIWON_YEAR = D.JIWON_YEAR
                                       AND E.JIWON_MM = D.JIWON_MM
                                       AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                       AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD')
                                     UNION 
                                    SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO 
                                      FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM IBC250MT
                                             WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                             GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                           ) C
                                         , IBB110MT D
                                         , IBB120MT E
                                     WHERE D.ILJARI_NO = C.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND C.JEOPSU_NO = E.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND D.ILJARI_NO         = E.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND D.JIWON_YEAR        = E.JIWON_YEAR
                                       AND D.JEONGGI_CNT       = E.JEONGGI_CNT
                                       AND D.JIWON_MM          = E.JIWON_MM
                                       AND D.SIMSA_CNT         = E.SIMSA_CNT
                                       AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                       AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD')
                                   ) AA
                             UNION ALL
                            SELECT '2'
                                 , BB.FBS_JIGEUP_DT AS DT
                                 , 0
                                 , COUNT(DISTINCT BB.ILJARI_NO ||BB.GEUNROJA_NO) AS DI_CNT
                                 , 0
                              FROM (SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO, C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                      FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM IBC250MT
                                             WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                             GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                           ) C
                                         , IBB010MT D
                                         , IBB020MT E
                                     WHERE D.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND E.JEOPSU_NO = D.JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND E.ILJARI_NO = D.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND E.JIWON_YEAR = D.JIWON_YEAR
                                       AND E.JIWON_MM = D.JIWON_MM
                                       AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                       AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT = TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD')
                                     UNION 
                                    SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO, C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT
                                      FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM IBC250MT
                                             WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                             GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                           ) C
                                         , IBB110MT D
                                         , IBB120MT E
                                     WHERE D.ILJARI_NO = C.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND C.JEOPSU_NO = E.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO
                                       AND D.ILJARI_NO         = E.ILJARI_NO
                                       AND D.JIWON_YEAR        = E.JIWON_YEAR
                                       AND D.JEONGGI_CNT       = E.JEONGGI_CNT
                                       AND D.JIWON_MM          = E.JIWON_MM
                                       AND D.SIMSA_CNT         = E.SIMSA_CNT
                                       AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                       AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT = TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD')
                                   ) BB                  
                             GROUP BY BB.FBS_JIGEUP_DT
                             UNION ALL
                            SELECT X.*
                              FROM (SELECT '3'
                                         , TO_CHAR(SYSDATE,'YYYYMMDD') AS DT
                                         , 0
                                         , 0
                                         , COUNT(DISTINCT PP.ILJARI_NO ||PP.GEUNROJA_NO) AS DI_CNT
                                      FROM (SELECT C.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO, C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                                      FROM IBC250MT
                                                     WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                                     GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                                   ) C
                                                 , IBB010MT D
                                                 , IBB020MT E
                                             WHERE D.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO
                                               AND E.JEOPSU_NO = D.JEOPSU_NO
                                               AND E.ILJARI_NO = D.ILJARI_NO
                                               AND E.JIWON_YEAR = D.JIWON_YEAR
                                               AND E.JIWON_MM = D.JIWON_MM
                                               AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                               AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE - 1,'YYYYMMDD')
                                             UNION 
                                            SELECT D.ILJARI_NO, E.GEUNROJA_NO, C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                              FROM (SELECT ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO, SUM(JIGEUP_PRC) AS JIGEUP_PRC, MIN(FBS_JIGEUP_DT) AS FBS_JIGEUP_DT 
                                                      FROM IBC250MT
                                                     WHERE FBS_JIGEUP_UIROE_FG = '2' AND FBS_JIGEUP_RESULT_CD = '0000' 
                                                     GROUP BY ILJARI_NO, JEOPSU_NO
                                                   ) C
                                                 , IBB110MT D
                                                 , IBB120MT E
                                             WHERE D.ILJARI_NO = C.ILJARI_NO
                                               AND C.JEOPSU_NO = E.JIGEUP_JEOPSU_NO
                                               AND D.ILJARI_NO         = E.ILJARI_NO
                                               AND D.JIWON_YEAR        = E.JIWON_YEAR
                                               AND D.JEONGGI_CNT       = E.JEONGGI_CNT
                                               AND D.JIWON_MM          = E.JIWON_MM
                                               AND D.SIMSA_CNT         = E.SIMSA_CNT
                                               AND E.JIWON_PRC_SANJENG_PRC > 0
                                               AND C.FBS_JIGEUP_DT <= TO_CHAR(SYSDATE - 1,'YYYYMMDD')
                                           ) PP
                                     GROUP BY PP.FBS_JIGEUP_DT
                                     ORDER BY PP.FBS_JIGEUP_DT DESC 
                                   ) X  
                             WHERE ROWNUM = 1
                             ) ZZ
                     GROUP BY ZZ.DT ) Y

                   , JEOPSU_NO
                   , BULSEUNGIN_SAYU_CD
                   , US_IOWN.SF_JB_JUNGGI_SOGEUP_JINHAENG(DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO, JIWON_YEAR, JEONGGI_CNT) AS SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD
                   , SIKBYEOL_NO
                   , DAMDANGJA_ID
                   , DAESANG_YN
                   , ROWNUM AS RNUM
                FROM (    
                      /* 구분 (정기심사) 조건시 */
                      SELECT /*+ ORDERED USE_INDEX_NL(B,C) */
                             DISTINCT A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO AS DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                           , A.ILJARI_NO
                           , A.GYB_GWANRI_NO
                           , A.SAEOPJANG_NM
                           , A.P_NM AS P_DAEPYOJA_NM
                           , CASE WHEN A.SAEOPJANG_FG IN ('2','3') THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N' END AS GONGDONGJUTAEK_YUHYEONG_CD
                           , A.DURUNURI_JIWON_YN
                           , A.SAEOPJA_DRNO
                           , A.JIGEUP_HUIMANG_IL
                           , A.GWANRI_JISA_CD
                           , A.JEOPSU_NO AS FIRST_JEOPSU_NO
                           , Q2.MINWON_DOC_CD AS FIRST_MINWON_DOC_CD
                           , B.SER
                           , B.CHANGE_JEOPSU_NO
                           , Q1.MINWON_DOC_CD AS CHANGE_MINWON_DOC_CD
                           , B.JAESIMSA_DAESANG_YN
                           , B.JAESIMSA_FG_CD
                           , B.JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_YN
                           , B.JAESIMSA_COMPLETE_DT
                           , B.JAESIMSA_JIGEUP_NO
                           , B.JIWON_JUNGJI_STATUS_CD
                           , B.JIWON_JUNGJI_SAYU_CD
                           , B.JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT
                           , B.JIWON_JUNGJI_HAEJI_DT
                           , C.JIWON_YEAR
                           , '' AS JIWON_MM
                           , C.JEONGGI_CNT
                           , C.SIMSA_CNT
                           , C.JEOPSU_NO
                           , '' AS BULSEUNGIN_SAYU_CD
                           , C.SIKBYEOL_NO
                           , E.JY_DAMDANGJA_ID AS DAMDANGJA_ID
                           , D.DAESANG_YN
                        FROM IAA190MT B
                        INNER JOIN IJB050MT C
                          ON C.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO  = B.ILJARI_NO
                         AND C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT = ? || ? || ?
                         AND C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT BETWEEN B.JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT AND B.JIWON_JUNGJI_HAEJI_DT  /* 2018.05.11 문형수K요청으로 조건추가 */
                       INNER JOIN IJB300MT D
                          ON D.GIJUN_DT        = C.JEONGGI_JIGEUP_DT
                        AND D.DAESANG_YN      IN ('S', 'J') /* 2018.04.23 문현수K 요청으로 Y 제거 */
                        AND D.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO       = C.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                          
                         
                         
                         AND C.SIMSA_CNT = (SELECT MAX(Y.SIMSA_CNT)
                                              FROM IJB050MT Y
                                             WHERE Y.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO   = C.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                                               AND Y.JIWON_YEAR  = C.JIWON_YEAR
                                               AND Y.JEONGGI_CNT = C.JEONGGI_CNT
                                           )
                        INNER JOIN IAA100MT A
                          ON A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO        = C.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                         AND A.ILJARI_NO               = C.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                         AND B.JIWON_JUNGJI_STATUS_CD  = '20'
                         AND B.JIWON_JUNGJI_SAYU_CD    = '200'
                         AND B.SER = (SELECT MAX(X.SER)
                                        FROM IAA190MT X
                                       WHERE X.ILJARI_NO = B.ILJARI_NO
                                         AND X.JIWON_JUNGJI_STATUS_CD  = '20'
                                         AND X.JIWON_JUNGJI_SAYU_CD    = '200'
                                         AND ? || ? || ? BETWEEN X.JIWON_JUNGJI_FROM_DT AND X.JIWON_JUNGJI_HAEJI_DT  /* 2018.05.11 문형수K요청으로 조건추가 */
                                     )
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN IQZ006MT E
                          ON E.ILJARI_NO    = A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN IQA500MT Q1
                          ON Q1.JEOPSU_NO = B.CHANGE_JEOPSU_NO
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN IQA500MT Q2
                          ON Q2.JEOPSU_NO = A.JEOPSU_NO
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN IQA500MT Q3
                          ON Q3.JEOPSU_NO = C.JEOPSU_NO
                       WHERE 1=1
                          
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                         
                       ORDER BY DECODE(SF_JB_JUNGGI_SOGEUP_GYEOLJAE(A.DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO, C.JIWON_YEAR, C.JEONGGI_CNT), '03', 1, '06', 2, '02', 3, '05', 4, '01', 5, '04', 6, 9)
                     ) A
               WHERE ROWNUM <= ?
             ) A
       WHERE RNUM >= ?

                   , JEOPSU_NO

                   , US_IOWN.SF_JB_JUNGGI_SOGEUP_JINHAENG(DAEPYO_ILJARI_NO, JIWON_YEAR, JEONGGI_CNT) AS SIMSA_JINHAENG_STATUS_CD

                           , A.DURUNURI_JIWON_YN
                           , A.SAEOPJA_DRNO
